shared_focus = {
	id = ZUG_my_name_is_amanyi
	icon = GFX_goal_unknown
	cost = 5
	x = 3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = ZUG_gods_great_lakes
	prerequisite = { focus = ZUG_the_great_council }
	prerequisite = { focus = ZUG_pride_in_king }
	prerequisite = { focus = ZUG_gods_great_lakes }
	prerequisite = { focus = ZUG_peaceful_kingdom }
	prerequisite = { focus = ZUG_stablized_economy }
	completion_reward = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ZUG_my_name_is_amanyi"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ZUG_amanyi_trait_explanation_tp
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ZUG_amanyi_ideology_variable < 4 }
			}
			country_event = { id = zugamanyi.28 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ZUG_amanyi_ideology_variable > 3 }
				check_variable = { ZUG_amanyi_ideology_variable < 7 }
			}
			country_event = { id = zugamanyi.29 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ZUG_amanyi_ideology_variable > 6 }
			}

	icon = GFX_goal_POL_recon_aircraft
	cost = 5
	x = 37
	y = 0

		NOT = {
			has_idea = agrarian_society
		}
	}

	completion_reward = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ZUG_purchase_planes"
		if = {
			limit = {
			    has_tech = early_fighter
		    }
		    add_tech_bonus = {
				name = early_fighter
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				technology = fighter1
				technology = fighter2
				technology = fighter3
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = fighter_equipment
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				early_fighter = 1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = fighter_equipment
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		964 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = air_base
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

### Military victory

shared_focus = {
	id = ZUG_begin_recruitment
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_drafted_army
	cost = 3
	x = 25
	y = 0

	available = {
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = ZUG_ugabi_god_nnabakyala
			has_government = democratic
		}
	}

	completion_reward = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ZUG_begin_recruitment"
		add_manpower = 14000
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }
			add_ideas = all_adults_serve
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = all_adults_serve }
			add_ideas = scraping_the_barrel
		}
	}
}

					}
				}

				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 950
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment
			amount = 400
		}
